Configuring slapd
-----------------

If you enable this option, no initial configuration or database will be created for you.

Omit OpenLDAP server configuration? [yes/no] n

The DNS domain name is used to construct the base DN of the LDAP directory. For example,
'foo.example.org' will create the directory with 'dc=foo, dc=example, dc=org' as base

Configuring slapd
-----------------

If you enable this option, no initial configuration or database will be created for you.

Omit OpenLDAP server configuration? [yes/no] n

The DNS domain name is used to construct the base DN of the LDAP directory. For example,
'foo.example.org' will create the directory with 'dc=foo, dc=example, dc=org' as base
DN.
